d_knights_saria = {
		color={ 177 60 100 }
		color2={ 255 255 23 }
	
	graphical_culture = holygfx

	capital = 196
	
	# Parent Religion 
	religion = golden_goddesses
	
	culture = sarian
	
	mercenary = yes

	title = "GRANDMASTER"
	foa = "GRANDMASTER_FOA"

	# Always exists
	landless = yes
	
	# Cannot be held as a secondary title
	primary = yes
	
	strength_growth_per_century = 0.10
	
	mercenary_type = knights_saria_composition
}
